ReddID REST API

Welcome

Welcome to the Reddcoin ReddID API. You can explore some of the functionality available

Overview

These examples serve as a starting point to help familiarise you with the workign of ReddID.

  • api/v1
    • status
    • consensus
    • names
    • name
  • api/v1/name
    • cost
    • preorder
    • register
    • update
    • profile
    • lookup
    • Names owned by address
  • api/v1/namespace
    • Namespace Names
    • Namespace Cost

api/v1 4

raw

status  |  GET   https://{{host}}/api/v1/status

Description

Returns the current server status

eg

https://{{host}}/api/v1/status


Response
Return the server status | Code: 200
{ "bitcoind_blocks": 2740753, "testset": "False", "last_block": 2740718, "indexing": false, "consensus": "b72d1a497e15157540370e867f6c5c5d", "blockstore_version": "0.0.12.1" }
raw

consensus  |  GET   https://{{host}}/api/v1/consensus

Description

Returns consensus with optional height

eg

https://{{host}}/api/v1/consensus?height={{height}}


Query
KeyValueDescription
height{{height}}

Height to query for consensus or remove to get latest

Response
Get consensus at current height | Code: 200
{ "consensus": "ec4f3b19d6dedcd50140af78292b0ff6", "height": 2700000 }
Get consensus at specified height | Code: 200
{ "consensus": "ec4f3b19d6dedcd50140af78292b0ff6", "height": 2600000 }
raw

names  |  GET   https://{{host}}/api/v1/names

Description

Returns all names in all blockspaces with optional offset and count

eg

https://{{host}}/api/v1/names?offset={{offset}}&count={{count}}


Query
KeyValueDescription
offset{{offset}}

Offset

count{{count}}

Count

Response
Return all names | Code: 200
